<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувяк.html>чувя́к</a> (29111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувяк.html>чувя́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čuvják</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувяк.html>чувя́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувяк.html>чувя́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувяк.html>чувя́ков</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувяк.html>чувя́к</a></strong></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a> (13261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chuvash_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chuvash language">Chuvash</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="cv"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čugun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">чуен</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">çuyen</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čugún</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугуна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугуны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугуно́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cast iron
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">séryj <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gray cast iron</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bélyj <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">white cast iron</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">переде́льный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">peredélʹnyj <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pig iron</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">чу́шковый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čúškovyj <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pig iron</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ко́вкий <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kóvkij <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">malleable iron</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cooking pot <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">traditionally made of cast iron</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-чугун-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чугунок.html>чугуно́к</a> (18560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čugún</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугунок.html>чугуно́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čugunók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугунок.html>чугунка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугунок.html>чугунки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугунок.html>чугунко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čugún</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (small, cast iron) pot, kettle, cauldron</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čudésnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čudésno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>miraculously, by a miracle</li>
<li>wonderfully, wonderful
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пахнуть.html>пахнут</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éti cvetý <b>čudésno</b> paxnut</i> ― <span class="e-translation">these flowers smell wonderful</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выглядеть.html>вы́глядишь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ty <b>čudésno</b> výgljadišʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you look wonderful</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čudésnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wonderful, miraculous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:избавление.html>избавле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čudésnoje</b> izbavlénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">miraculous escape</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>wonderful, lovely, beautiful, marvellous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>čudésnyj</b> vid</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he looks wonderful/splendid</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудиться.html>чу́диться</a> (7911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čuditi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудиться.html>чу́диться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúditʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почудиться.html>почу́диться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem <i>(to)</i>, to appear <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудиться.html>чу́дится</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>čúditsja</b>, što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it seems to him that; he seems to see (hear) that; he imagines that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудиться.html>чу́дится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стук.html>стук</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>čúditsja</b> stuk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he seems to hear (it seems to him that he hears) a knock</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чу́до</a> (1023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čudo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чу́до</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúdo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чу́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чудеса́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чуде́с</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>miracle, marvel</li>
<li>wonder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:семь.html>семь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чуде́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">semʹ čudés svéta</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Seven Wonders of the World</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чу.html>чу</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зе́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>мец</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чум.html>чума</a> (13019)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чум.html>чума́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čumá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чум.html>чумы́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>plague, pestilence</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">specifically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the plague, the Black Death</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***чумазый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чумазый.html>чума́зый</a> (16827)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чу-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ču-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (unclear) + the root of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mázatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to soil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чумазый.html>чума́зый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čumázyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чума́зее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чума́зей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dirty, stained</li></ol>
